        html += '<div class="g-plusone" data-annotation="none" data-href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/+snapdeal/posts"></div>';
        html += "<a href='http://pinterest.com/Snapdeal/' title='Follow Me on Pinterest' class='followMePin' >Follow Me on Pinterest</a></div>";
		html += '<div class="clear"></div>';
		$('.footerShareLinks').html(html);
        var deferedScript = $("#deferredFooterScript").html().replace("<!--COMMENTSTARTED", "").replace("COMMENTENDED-->", "");
        deferedScript = decodeURIComponent(deferedScript.replace(/\+/g, '%20'));
        $("#deferredFooterScript").html(deferedScript);
	}
	var oldonload = window.onload;
	var firstHit = document.getElementById("firstHit").getAttribute("u");
	if(firstHit == "firstHit") {
		loadFooterFiles();
	}else {
		window.onload = function() {
		setTimeout(function(){
				loadFooterFiles();
			},10)
		};
	}

})();
